# Page 3
Government Resolution No: SEVAPR 2019/ PR No.194/ KHASA-3
Instructions have been given to review the sanctioned posts at the establishment and fix the revised figure with the approval of the high-level secretary committee.
Subordinate Directorate of Accounts and Treasuries and Subordinate Offices of the Finance Department
The required posts are to be reviewed as per the Government Decision dated 18th August 2008 of the Finance Department.
A total of 4632 posts in Maharashtra Finance and Accounts Service (including 132 posts in Maharashtra Finance and Accounts Service Cadre in Zilla Parishads) in various cadres and Govt. from time to time.
Out of the total 163 sanctioned posts, a total of 4,795 posts are sanctioned, including 4,659 in the Directorate and Subordinate Offices and 136 in the Maharashtra Finance and Accounts Service Cadre in the Zilla Parishads.
However, the change in the nature and scale of work of the Treasuries and Sub-Treasuries as well as the Subordinate and Accounts Offices during the last seven to eight years has led to a change in the nature and scale of work.
Keeping in view the increasing use of computerization, it was necessary to change the existing structure of the Directorate. Accordingly, the posts in the Directorate of Accounts and Treasuries, Mumbai, Headquarters, Divisional, District and Taluk level offices as well as other field offices under them will be transferred to the Government Decision, Finance Department. as on 09.06.2017. With the approval of the Sub-Committee and Scrutiny Committee formed under the chairmanship of Additional Chief Secretary (Services), General Administration Department, regularization- 4007, on the establishment of Zila Parishad- 136, new posts- 337
A total of 4480 posts and the total number of manpower to be recruited by external agencies- 134. The high-level committee is headed by the Chief Secretary. dated 23.08.2021
This was approved in the meeting.

GOVERNMENT DECISIONS: The Government have accorded approval to revise the profile of the Directorate, Accounts and Treasuries, Mumbai and its Subordinate Regional Offices with the approval of the High Level Committee of Secretaries as under: (a) The consolidated statement of accounts showing the office-wise sanctioned posts as per the revised profile in the Directorate, Accounts and Treasuries and Subordinate Offices and the details of the 4480 posts in the Directorate, Accounts and Treasuries, Mumbai and its Subordinate Regional Offices and the number of manpower to be recruited through external agencies 134 to be added as shown in Annexure-A.
